[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m104[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.tika.parser.threedxml.ThreeDXMLParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mThreeDXMLParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:86[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.example.ThreeDXMLParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mThreeDXMLParserFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:39[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: f8a914f52bb68598[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability has been detected in the Apache [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTika ThreeDXMLParser during fuzz testing. The parser attempted an unauthorized [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnection to an external domain [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when processing XML content, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating that the parser processes external entity references without proper [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation or restrictions. This vulnerability could potentially allow attackers to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexfiltrate sensitive data or probe internal network services.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** vulnerability, classified as a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmedium severity security issue. SSRF vulnerabilities occur when an application [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmakes requests to arbitrary destinations based on untrusted input, potentially [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallowing attackers to interact with internal systems or external resources in [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munintended ways.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Observable Behavior[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe stack trace reveals that during XML parsing operations within the [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThreeDXMLParser, the system attempted to establish an HTTPS connection to [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[39m. The connection attempt was initiated through the following [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequence:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The ThreeDXMLParser was processing a ZIP file containing 3D XML content[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. During XML parsing, the SAXParser encountered an entity reference[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The XMLEntityManager attempted to resolve this entity reference by accessing an [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal resource[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. This triggered a network connection attempt through Java's HttpsURLConnection[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. The SSRF detection mechanism intercepted the connection attempt at the socket [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlevel[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Technical Flow[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests through the following call chain:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mThreeDXMLParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;35mparseContent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;35mprocessZip[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;35mparseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The parseRoot method uses `[0m[1;35mSAXParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to process XML content[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The XML parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`XMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m encounters and attempts to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolve an entity reference[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `[0m[1;35mXMLEntityManager.startEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method initiates a connection to fetch the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal entity[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This results in an HTTPS connection attempt to the external domain[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Findings[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **XML External Entity Processing**: The ThreeDXMLParser uses a SAXParser that is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfigured to resolve external entities, allowing XML documents to reference and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfetch external resources.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No Input Validation**: There appears to be no validation or sanitization of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity references in the XML content before attempting to resolve them.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Network Access During Parsing**: The parser has unrestricted network access [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcapabilities, allowing it to make outbound connections based on XML content.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **ZIP File Processing**: The vulnerability occurs during the processing of ZIP [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchives, specifically when parsing XML files contained within them [0m[1;39m([0m[39mas indicated [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby the `[0m[1;35mprocessZip[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method in the stack trace[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo obtain a comprehensive understanding of this vulnerability, the following [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents should be examined:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **ThreeDXMLParser Configuration** [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`org.apache.tika.parser.threedxml.ThreeDXMLParser`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mparseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method at line [0m[1;36m141[0m[39m where [0m[1;35mSAXParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is invoked[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mprocessZip[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method at line [0m[1;36m120[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mparseContent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method at line [0m[1;36m104[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How the SAXParser instance is created and configured[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **SAXParser Configuration**:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether features like `FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING` are enabled[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Settings for `XMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Configuration of external entity resolution [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`disallow-doctype-decl`, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`external-general-entities`, `external-parameter-entities`[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **XML Entity Resolution**:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How the XMLEntityManager handles external entity references[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether there are any entity resolvers configured[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - What restrictions, if any, are placed on entity resolution[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Input Processing Pipeline**:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How ZIP files are extracted and processed[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - What validation occurs before XML parsing[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether there are any content security policies applied[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Related Parsers**:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other XML-based parsers in the Tika codebase that might share similar [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfigurations[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Common XML parsing utilities or factory methods used across the codebase[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis vulnerability represents a classic XML External Entity [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXXE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m attack vector [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat has escalated to SSRF, where malicious XML content can trigger the application[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto make requests to arbitrary network destinations.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis Summary[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I've identified the root [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the SSRF vulnerability in the Apache Tika ThreeDXMLParser:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `[0m[1;35mparseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method in ThreeDXMLParser [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m123[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m143[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m creates an insecure [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXParser directly without configuring any security features to prevent XXE/SSRF [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattacks. Specifically:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m129[0m[39m: Creates `[0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` without security configuration[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m130[0m[39m: Only sets `[0m[1;35msetNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` - no security features[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m141[0m[39m: Parses XML directly with the insecure parser, allowing external entity [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolution[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Findings[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Inconsistency**: The same class already uses `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurely for Manifest.xml [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m118[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but bypasses it for root XML parsing[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Pattern Match**: The vulnerable code exactly matches the `VulnerableSAXParser`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLTestBase.java lines [0m[1;36m144[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m147[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m used to demonstrate XXE [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerabilities[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Missing Protections**: No external entity blocking, no DTD restrictions, no [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity expansion limits, no OfflineContentHandler wrapper[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Required Security Features [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfrom XMLReaderUtils[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING` enabled[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `external-general-entities` disabled[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `external-parameter-entities` disabled[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `load-external-dtd` disabled[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `load-dtd-grammar` disabled[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Entity expansion limits via Xerces SecurityManager[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- OfflineContentHandler wrapper to block entity resolution at handler level[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Replace Insecure Parsing with XMLReaderUtils[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-cad-m[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/threedxml/ThreeDXMLParser.java`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes to `[0m[1;35mparseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m123[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m143[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Remove insecure SAXParser creation** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m129[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m137[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete `SAXParserFactory factory = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete `[0m[1;35mfactory.setNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete the try-catch block that creates `parser = [0m[1;35mfactory.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Replace insecure parsing call** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m141[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace `[0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - With `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Remove unused imports** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m25[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m27[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove `import javax.xml.parsers.ParserConfigurationException;`[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove `import javax.xml.parsers.SAXParser;`[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove `import javax.xml.parsers.SAXParserFactory;`[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Resulting Secure Implementation[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fixed `[0m[1;35mparseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method should look like:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate void [0m[1;35mparseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString root, ZipFile zipFile, ContentHandler handler, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMetadata metadata,[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                       ParseContext context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws SAXException, IOException, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTikaException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ZipArchiveEntry rootEntry = [0m[1;35mzipFile.getEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[39mroot[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrootEntry == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    RootHandler rootHandler = new [0m[1;35mRootHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandler, metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mzipFile.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrootEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Consistency**: Makes [0m[1;35mparseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m consistent with [0m[1;35mprocessZip[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m118[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready uses [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Simplicity**: Reduces code complexity by removing [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m lines of insecure parser [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreation[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Defense in Depth**: Automatically applies multiple security layers:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - SAXParserFactory configuration with all security features disabled[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Xerces SecurityManager for entity expansion limits[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - OfflineContentHandler wrapper that returns empty streams for any entity [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolution[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Proven Pattern**: Uses the same secure pattern as [0m[1;35mXMLParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m74[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and other Tika XML parsers[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **RootHandler Compatibility**: The RootHandler extends DefaultHandler and is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfully compatible with [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Functionality Preserved**: All metadata extraction and content forwarding [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic in RootHandler remains unchanged[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Test Compatibility**: The existing test [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mThreeDXMLParserTest.testBasic[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to pass as the parsing behavior is preserved, only security is enhanced[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes**: The method signature and exception handling remain the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msame[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Addresses Security Issues[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Blocks SSRF**: XMLReaderUtils disables external entity resolution, preventing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnections to external domains[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Prevents XXE**: Multiple layers of protection against XML External Entity [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattacks[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Entity Expansion Limits**: Prevents billion laughs and similar attacks[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Consistent Security Posture**: Aligns with Tika's security best practices used[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthroughout the codebase[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects**: [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected, as:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix only enhances security without changing parsing behavior[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- RootHandler processes the same SAX events regardless of parser configuration[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- External entities in 3DXML files would be a security vulnerability anyway, so [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblocking them is intended behavior[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Testing**: The existing test suite should pass without modification, as [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegitimate 3DXML files don't rely on external entities.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix follows the exact pattern used by:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **XMLParser** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtika-parser-xml-module[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Uses [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for all [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXML parsing[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **FictionBookParser**: Extends XMLParser to leverage secure parsing[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **DcXMLParser**: Extends XMLParser to leverage secure parsing[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **ThreeDXMLParser's own [0m[1;35mprocessZip[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Already uses [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor Manifest.xml [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m118[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix makes [0m[1;35mparseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m consistent with the established secure pattern used [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthroughout the Tika codebase.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
